# Leveraging AI in Adobe Photoshop and Creative Cloud (2023)

> The Adobe Creative Cloud tools are filled with time-saving, creativity-enhancing features built on a foundation of artificial intelligence. Whether it's making masking easier in Photoshop and Lightroom, editing in Illustrator, or matching similar fonts in InDesign, the AI features in the Creative Cloud apps are "creativity copilots" that simplify tedious tasks and enable you to concentrate on crea

### 1. The Role of Artificial Intelligence in Your Workflows

#### Welcome to the age of artificial intelligence
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/welcome-to-the-age-of-artificial-intelligence?u=76281980)

>
> **[0:20](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/welcome-to-the-age-of-artificial-intelligence?u=76281980&t=20)** And the thing is, you will probably not even notice that whatever feature you're using is driven by AI or a machine learning model.

>
> **[0:53](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/welcome-to-the-age-of-artificial-intelligence?u=76281980&t=53)** Now these tools help you facilitate, or even automate, very specific tasks that would normally cost you a lot of time.

>
> **[1:03](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/welcome-to-the-age-of-artificial-intelligence?u=76281980&t=63)** So many of us have been using this feature for many years now, and we would almost forget that it is AI in the background that helps us fuel that feature and gives us the result that we now see today.
>
> **[1:15](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/welcome-to-the-age-of-artificial-intelligence?u=76281980&t=75)** The second evolution is the rise of powerful design tools for non-designers, for example, Adobe Express.
>
> **[1:22](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/welcome-to-the-age-of-artificial-intelligence?u=76281980&t=82)** Now you might think, "What does Adobe Express have to do with artificial intelligence?"
>
> **[1:28](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/welcome-to-the-age-of-artificial-intelligence?u=76281980&t=88)** Well, let's think about auto styling for a second.

>
> **[1:40](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/welcome-to-the-age-of-artificial-intelligence?u=76281980&t=100)** By opening up these AI tools via the interface of a simple web browser, you can have people who didn't go to design school for two or three years and still create powerful designs using a very simple interface and a template-based system.

>
> **[2:04](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/welcome-to-the-age-of-artificial-intelligence?u=76281980&t=124)** Now, at the time of this recording, Adobe Firefly is still in a public beta.
>

>
> **[2:21](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/welcome-to-the-age-of-artificial-intelligence?u=76281980&t=141)** Now there's a lot more functionality on its way, but today we're going to focus on Adobe Sensei, which drives all of the AI features that come out of the box when you install Adobe Creative Cloud.

> **[2:32](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/welcome-to-the-age-of-artificial-intelligence?u=76281980&t=152)** Let's take a look.

#### Introducing Adobe Sensei
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/introducing-adobe-sensei?u=76281980)

> [!transcript]- Transcript
>
> **[0:01](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/introducing-adobe-sensei?u=76281980&t=1)** - Let's talk about Adobe Sensei for a few minutes.
>
> **[0:03](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/introducing-adobe-sensei?u=76281980&t=3)** It's important for you to know what Adobe Sensei is or isn't, how Adobe describes Adobe Sensei and what that means to you as a Creative Cloud user.
>
> **[0:13](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/introducing-adobe-sensei?u=76281980&t=13)** Now, Adobe describes Adobe Sensei as something that brings the power of AI and machine learning to experiences, deepening insights, enhancing creative expression, accelerating tasks and workflows, and driving real time decisions.
>
> **[0:29](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/introducing-adobe-sensei?u=76281980&t=29)** Now, it's important here to realize that this is first of all, a lot of information, and secondly, that Adobe Sensei is not a product, it's not something you simply install on your hard drive.
>
> **[0:40](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/introducing-adobe-sensei?u=76281980&t=40)** And on top of that, Adobe Sensei is bigger than Adobe Creative Cloud alone.
>
> **[0:45](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/introducing-adobe-sensei?u=76281980&t=45)** And what many people often forget is that Adobe is a company that has three major clouds in its portfolio.
>
> **[0:52](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/introducing-adobe-sensei?u=76281980&t=52)** The first one is Adobe Creative Cloud that I'm sure you're familiar with.
>
> **[0:56](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/introducing-adobe-sensei?u=76281980&t=56)** Now, Adobe Sensei is able to assist or fuel Creative Cloud features by offering image analysis services, font managing technology or color analysis.
>
> **[1:07](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/introducing-adobe-sensei?u=76281980&t=67)** The second one is Adobe Document Cloud.
>
> **[1:09](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/introducing-adobe-sensei?u=76281980&t=69)** And if you're using apps like Adobe Acrobat, I'm sure you're familiar with Document Cloud.
>
> **[1:14](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/introducing-adobe-sensei?u=76281980&t=74)** So Adobe Sensei is helping the Document Cloud solutions, for example, by fueling form field recognitions when you're creating interactive forms, but also by means of cleaning up an image whenever you take a picture of an image using the Adobe Scan application.
>
> **[1:29](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/introducing-adobe-sensei?u=76281980&t=89)** And then the last one is the Adobe Experience Cloud, Adobe's bundle of digital marketing tools, where Adobe Sensei is used to help auto tag images that you add to a database so you can easily find them again, or anomaly detection where you can detect when a customer starts to show a different type of online shopping behavior, or general data mining and insights whenever you're analyzing the profile of one of your digital customers.
>
> **[1:56](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/introducing-adobe-sensei?u=76281980&t=116)** Let's illustrate what we've just learned by just showing a very basic example.
>
> **[2:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/introducing-adobe-sensei?u=76281980&t=120)** Here's the example of the infamous Content-Aware Fill in Photoshop.
>
> **[2:04](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/introducing-adobe-sensei?u=76281980&t=124)** Now, first of all, we have to make a selection, and here we can use an auto selecting method using the Object selection tool in Photoshop, a tool that you'll learn throughout this course.
>
> **[2:15](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/introducing-adobe-sensei?u=76281980&t=135)** Now, the Object Selection tool allows you to basically select a subject in a picture, and it is Adobe Sensei that will automatically detect that subject by recognizing that this is a different object within a pattern in the background.
>
> **[2:30](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/introducing-adobe-sensei?u=76281980&t=150)** So clearly these two kids are sticking out if you look at the background sea, secondly, a selection is created, and lastly, that selection needs to be filled up by extending the pattern that found in the background, keeping in mind that there's a sharp line for the waves, the foam in the water and then the rest of the background.
>
> **[2:50](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/introducing-adobe-sensei?u=76281980&t=170)** So by analyzing the image, recognizing patterns and learning what is a potential subject in a picture and what is not, Sensei can help you try better results in various applications, or like in this case, Adobe Photoshop.

#### The role of Adobe Sensei in Creative Cloud
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/the-role-of-adobe-sensei-in-creative-cloud?u=76281980)

>
> **[0:01](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/the-role-of-adobe-sensei-in-creative-cloud?u=76281980&t=1)** - Now that we know what Adobe Sensei is, let's take a minute to talk about why Adobe Sensei exists.
>
> **[0:06](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/the-role-of-adobe-sensei-in-creative-cloud?u=76281980&t=6)** The short answer is workload.
>
> **[0:09](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/the-role-of-adobe-sensei-in-creative-cloud?u=76281980&t=9)** We are busy bees, and the demands of customers has just been increasing the last couple of years.
>
> **[0:15](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/the-role-of-adobe-sensei-in-creative-cloud?u=76281980&t=15)** If you were an all-around graphic designer just a couple years ago, there's a good chance that you're now a graphic designer and a photographer.
>
> **[0:22](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/the-role-of-adobe-sensei-in-creative-cloud?u=76281980&t=22)** If you were a photographer, then maybe you're now a photographer and a videographer.
>
> **[0:26](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/the-role-of-adobe-sensei-in-creative-cloud?u=76281980&t=26)** If you were an illustrator, then maybe you're now also doing animations of your illustrations.
>
> **[0:31](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/the-role-of-adobe-sensei-in-creative-cloud?u=76281980&t=31)** We have a lot more demands for content, and that is driving the need to upscale a lot quicker, but also to scale up the amount of content that we have to create.
>
> **[0:42](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/the-role-of-adobe-sensei-in-creative-cloud?u=76281980&t=42)** But we don't always have time for this.
>
> **[0:45](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/the-role-of-adobe-sensei-in-creative-cloud?u=76281980&t=45)** There was a recent survey conducted by Adobe and [cmo.com](https://cmo.com) where 74% of the creatives they interviewed told them that they spent more than 50% of their time on non-creative tasks.
>
> **[0:59](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/the-role-of-adobe-sensei-in-creative-cloud?u=76281980&t=59)** Now, what are non-creative tasks?
>
> **[1:02](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/the-role-of-adobe-sensei-in-creative-cloud?u=76281980&t=62)** It is replacing images.
>
> **[1:04](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/the-role-of-adobe-sensei-in-creative-cloud?u=76281980&t=64)** It is making updates to icons by simply changing a color.
>
> **[1:08](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/the-role-of-adobe-sensei-in-creative-cloud?u=76281980&t=68)** It is making selections over and over again or repeating all sort sorts of tasks in various applications.
>
> **[1:15](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/the-role-of-adobe-sensei-in-creative-cloud?u=76281980&t=75)** So there are clearly tasks that you can give to AI to help you accelerate these processes.
>
> **[1:21](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/the-role-of-adobe-sensei-in-creative-cloud?u=76281980&t=81)** Let's take a look at a few examples.
>
> **[1:24](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/the-role-of-adobe-sensei-in-creative-cloud?u=76281980&t=84)** Here are five basic examples of how Sensei can help you in your day-to-day workflow.
>
> **[1:29](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/the-role-of-adobe-sensei-in-creative-cloud?u=76281980&t=89)** And just so you know, you will be learning all five of these methods once you finish this course.
>
> **[1:34](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/the-role-of-adobe-sensei-in-creative-cloud?u=76281980&t=94)** So this is about automatically selecting and masking objects and images using Adobe Lightroom, or fine-tuning selections when you're selecting hairs in Photoshop, or how about automatically detecting, and selecting, and editing shapes that look similar to one another in Illustrator?
>
> **[1:53](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/the-role-of-adobe-sensei-in-creative-cloud?u=76281980&t=113)** Now there are multiple advantages linked to using Sensei-driven features.
>
> **[1:58](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/the-role-of-adobe-sensei-in-creative-cloud?u=76281980&t=118)** The first advantage is saving time.
>
> **[2:01](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/the-role-of-adobe-sensei-in-creative-cloud?u=76281980&t=121)** You will have the ability to finish certain tasks a lot quicker.
>
> **[2:05](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/the-role-of-adobe-sensei-in-creative-cloud?u=76281980&t=125)** If you used to spend 15 minutes on a very complex selection, maybe you'll now spend three minutes on a very complex selection.
>
> **[2:12](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/the-role-of-adobe-sensei-in-creative-cloud?u=76281980&t=132)** When you finish earlier, when you save time throughout your day or throughout your week, you will have the ability to ideate faster, creative additional versions for the same design, you can take your project and get it approved faster, or even go to print or go to publish a lot quicker than before.
>
> **[2:30](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/the-role-of-adobe-sensei-in-creative-cloud?u=76281980&t=150)** Secondly, there is an improvement of quality.
>
> **[2:34](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/the-role-of-adobe-sensei-in-creative-cloud?u=76281980&t=154)** You will be able to do things in a better or higher level of quality than you were able to do before, or maybe even achieve things that were just very challenging for you from a technical point of view.
>
> **[2:45](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/the-role-of-adobe-sensei-in-creative-cloud?u=76281980&t=165)** And thirdly, this will also lower the threshold.
>

> **[2:28](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/selecting-objects?u=76281980&t=148)** Now this means that there's information of your image sent to the cloud, to an algorithm that runs online in Adobe's cloud and then it will send you back that selection, which means that when you use the select command, there might be a one or two second delay as you use that command.

### 6. Using AI in Adobe Stock

#### Introducing Adobe Stock
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/introducing-adobe-stock?u=76281980)

> [!transcript]- Transcript
>
> **[0:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/introducing-adobe-stock?u=76281980&t=0)** - [Instructor] Let's talk about Adobe Stock for a few minutes.
>
> **[0:03](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/introducing-adobe-stock?u=76281980&t=3)** Adobe Stock is a subscription-based asset database to which you can subscribe as a marketer or graphic designer.
>
> **[0:09](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/introducing-adobe-stock?u=76281980&t=9)** And Adobe has given Adobe Stock a lot of love and attention these last few years for various reason.

> **[0:27](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/introducing-adobe-stock?u=76281980&t=27)** And companies are struggling with the exact same issue as made clear through various studies conducted by Adobe and [cmo.com](https://cmo.com).

> **[0:53](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/introducing-adobe-stock?u=76281980&t=53)** Now Adobe Stock is a massive database of hundreds of millions of different assets and not just images.
>
> **[1:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/introducing-adobe-stock?u=76281980&t=60)** There are images, there are vector illustrations, videos, 3D assets, audio, and templates.

> **[1:08](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/introducing-adobe-stock?u=76281980&t=68)** So this means that you have a variety of ready to go templates for using InDesign, Photoshop, Illustrator, or Premiere Pro which means that you don't really have to start your design with a blank screen.
>
> **[1:21](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/introducing-adobe-stock?u=76281980&t=81)** Now, obviously it is up to you to personalize and change whatever it is you want to change.

>
> **[1:31](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/introducing-adobe-stock?u=76281980&t=91)** Now, what makes Adobe Stock special?
>
> **[1:33](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/introducing-adobe-stock?u=76281980&t=93)** Why is this relevant to this course in the first place?

> **[1:36](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/introducing-adobe-stock?u=76281980&t=96)** Well, there are two major things that make Adobe Stock special.
>
> **[1:39](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/introducing-adobe-stock?u=76281980&t=99)** First of all, keep in mind that when you're using artificial intelligence or machine learning, you need to have a point of reference.
>
> **[1:46](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/introducing-adobe-stock?u=76281980&t=106)** Now, in the case of Adobe Sensei, Adobe Sensei is also trained using the Adobe Stock database, which means that from a machine learning point of view, Adobe stock is strategically important to Adobe.
>
> **[1:58](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/introducing-adobe-stock?u=76281980&t=118)** Secondly, there is the Creative Cloud integration.
>
> **[2:02](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/introducing-adobe-stock?u=76281980&t=122)** What makes Stock interesting is the fact that you can safely save previews to a shared Creative Cloud library as so.
>
> **[2:09](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/introducing-adobe-stock?u=76281980&t=129)** And by saving that image here into the library, you can use that directly in any Creative Cloud application to help you boost your production workflow.
>
> **[2:18](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/introducing-adobe-stock?u=76281980&t=138)** And the moment you license and use that image inside of a project, like you see here inside of Adobe InDesign, you have the ability to license the image once and you will see that update occur across all of the projects where this library is linked to.
>
> **[2:32](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/introducing-adobe-stock?u=76281980&t=152)** Now what's interesting here for this particular course is the fact that you have AI-based search capabilities built into Adobe stock, and you will find out about all these features in the next couple of videos.
>
> **[2:45](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/introducing-adobe-stock?u=76281980&t=165)** So this includes different smart filters that help you describe the look and feel of an image instead of just simply using keywords, an image-based search system where you can input your own image as the basis to find additional images in combination with filters and keywords, and a very unique subject-aware search.
>
> **[3:05](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/leveraging-ai-in-adobe-photoshop-and-creative-cloud-2023/introducing-adobe-stock?u=76281980&t=185)** Now you've already discovered the select subject command in Photoshop or the select subject command when you're working in InDesign and you're applying text wrap.
